create table public."Account"(
	"username" varchar(20),
	"password" varchar(20),
	"accountType" int,
	"token" varchar(200),
	primary key (username)
);

	"MaTinhTP" varchar(8),

	"MaNQL" varchar(8),
	"HoTen" varchar(50),
	"CMND/CCCD" varchar(12),
	"NgaySinh" date,
	"GioiTinh" varchar(4),
	"DiaChi" varchar(50),
	"MaPhuongXa" varchar(8),
	"username" varchar(20),
	primary key ("MaNQL")
);

create table public."LichSuHoatDong"(
	"MaLSHD" varchar(8),
	"HoatDong" varchar(100),
	"ThoiGian" timestamp,
	"MaNQL" varchar(8),
	primary key ("MaLSHD")
);




create table public."NguoiLienQuanCovid"(
	"MaNLQ" varchar(8),
	"HoTen" varchar(50),
	"CMND/CCCD" varchar(12),
	"NgaySinh" date,
	"GioiTinh" varchar(4),
	"DiaChi" varchar(50),
	"MaPhuongXa" varchar(8),
	"MaNLQTruoc" varchar(8),
	"username" varchar(20),
	primary key ("MaNLQ")
);

create table public."LichSuTrangThai"(
	"STT" int,
	"MaNQL" varchar(8),
	"TrangThai" int,
	"NgayTao" timestamp,
	primary key ("STT","MaNQL")
);





-- insert LichSuTrangThai
create or replace procedure insertLichSuTrangThai()
language plpgsql    
as $$
declare Ma varchar(8);
		numb char;
		status int;
	 	cur cursor for select "MaNLQ" from public."NguoiLienQuanCovid";
begin
    open cur;
	fetch next from cur into Ma;
	loop 
		numb := SUBSTRING ( Ma ,7 , 1 );
		if (numb = '1' or numb = '8') then  status := 0; 
 			elseif (numb = '2' or numb = '3' or numb = '9') then status := 1; 
 				else  status := 2;
 		end if;
		insert into public."LichSuTrangThai" values (1, Ma, status, current_timestamp);
		fetch next from cur into Ma;
		exit when not found;
	end loop;
	close cur;
end;$$;

call insertLichSuTrangThai();





create table public."TaiKhoanThanhToan"(
	"MaTKTT" varchar(8),
	"SoDu" int,
	"HanMucToiThieu" int,
	primary key ("MaTKTT")
);



-- insert TaiKhoanThanhToan
create or replace procedure insertTaiKhoanThanhToan()
language plpgsql    
as $$
declare Ma varchar(8);
		stt char(4);
		newKey varchar(8);
	 	cur cursor for select "MaNLQ" from public."NguoiLienQuanCovid";
begin
    open cur;
	fetch next from cur into Ma;
	loop 
		stt := SUBSTRING ( Ma ,4 , 4 );
		newKey := 'TKTT'|| stt;
		insert into public."TaiKhoanThanhToan" values (newKey, 0, 1000);
		fetch next from cur into Ma;
		exit when not found;
	end loop;
	close cur;
end;$$;

call insertTaiKhoanThanhToan();

	"MaSP" varchar(8),
	"TenSP" varchar(50),
	"GiaTien" int,
	"DonViDinhLuong" varchar(50),
	"SoLuong" int,
	primary key ("MaSP")
);

create table public."HinhAnhSP"(
	"MaHASP" varchar(8),
	"url" varchar(200),
	"MaSP" varchar(8),
	primary key ("MaHASP")
);

-- insert HinhAnhSP
create or replace procedure insertHinhAnhSP()
language plpgsql    
as $$
declare Ma varchar(8);
		stt char(4);
		newKey varchar(8);
	 	cur cursor for select "MaSP" from public."SanPham";
begin
    open cur;
	fetch next from cur into Ma;
	loop 
		stt := SUBSTRING ( Ma ,3 , 3 );
		newKey := 'HASP'|| stt;
		insert into public."HinhAnhSP" values (newKey, null, Ma);
		fetch next from cur into Ma;
		exit when not found;
	end loop;
	close cur;
end;$$;

call insertHinhAnhSP();

 




create table public."GoiNhuYeuPham"(
	"MaNYP" varchar(8),
	"TenGoi" varchar(50),
	"GioiHanGoi/Nguoi" int,
	"ThoiGianGioiHan" int,
	primary key ("MaNYP")
);

create table public."ChiTietNhuYeuPham"(
	"MaCTNYP" int NOT NULL GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY ( INCREMENT 1 START 1 MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 2147483647 CACHE 1 ),
	"GioiHanSL" int,
	"SoLuong" int,
	"MaNYP" varchar(8),
	"MaSP" varchar(8),
	primary key ("MaCTNYP")
);

insert into public."ChiTietNhuYeuPham"("GioiHanSL", "SoLuong", "MaNYP", "MaSP") values (10, 1, 'NYP001', 'SP003');


create table public."DonHang"(
	"MaDH" varchar(8),
	"TongTien" varchar(50),
	"ThoiGian" timestamp,
	"MaNLQ" varchar(8),
	"MaNYP" varchar(8),
	primary key ("MaDH")
);


create table public."ChiTietDonHang"(
	"MaCTDH" int NOT NULL GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY ( INCREMENT 1 START 1 MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 2147483647 CACHE 1 ),
	"MaDH" varchar(8),
	"MaSP" varchar(8),
	"SoLuong" int,
	primary key ("MaCTDH")
);






-- update khoa ngoai username trong NguoiLienQuan
create or replace procedure updateUserNguoiLienQuan()
language plpgsql    
as $$
declare Ma varchar(8);
	 	cur cursor for select "MaNLQ" from public."NguoiLienQuanCovid";
begin
    open cur;
	fetch next from cur into Ma;
	loop 
		-- adding the amount to the receiver's account
		update public."NguoiLienQuanCovid"
		set "username" = Ma 
		where "MaNLQ" = Ma;
		fetch next from cur into Ma;
		exit when not found;
	end loop;
	close cur;
    

end;$$;

call updateUserNguoiLienQuan();



-- update khoa ngoai username trong NguoiQuanLy
create or replace procedure updateUserNguoiQuanLy()
language plpgsql    
as $$
declare Ma varchar(8);
	 	cur cursor for select "MaNQL" from public."NguoiQuanLy";
begin
    open cur;
	fetch next from cur into Ma;
	loop 
		-- adding the amount to the receiver's account
		update public."NguoiQuanLy"
		set "username" = Ma 
		where "MaNQL" = Ma;
		fetch next from cur into Ma;
		exit when not found;
	end loop;
	close cur;
    

end;$$;

call updateUserNguoiQuanLy();


-- create Account NguoiQuanLy
create or replace procedure createAccountNguoiQuanLy()
language plpgsql    
as $$
declare Ma varchar(8);
		CMND varchar(12);
	 	cur cursor for select "MaNQL","CMND/CCCD" from public."NguoiQuanLy";
begin
    open cur;
	fetch next from cur into Ma,CMND;
	loop 
		-- adding the amount to the receiver's account
		insert into public."Account" values (Ma,CMND,1,null);
		fetch next from cur into Ma,CMND;
		exit when not found;
	end loop;
	close cur;
    

end;$$;

call createAccountNguoiQuanLy();


-- create Account NguoiLienQuan
create or replace procedure createAccountNguoiLienQuan()
language plpgsql    
as $$
declare Ma varchar(8);
		CMND varchar(12);
	 	cur cursor for select "MaNLQ","CMND/CCCD" from public."NguoiLienQuanCovid";
begin
    open cur;
	fetch next from cur into Ma,CMND;
	loop 
		-- adding the amount to the receiver's account
		insert into public."Account" values (Ma,CMND,2,null);
		fetch next from cur into Ma,CMND;
		exit when not found;
	end loop;
	close cur;

end;$$;

call createAccountNguoiLienQuan();
